Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori Te whakamātau tōmua i te hunga e haere mai ana ki Aotearoa | Pre-departure testing for travellers to New Zealand --- Section Separator --- Ko te pare atu i te mate korona i Aotearoa, te mahi tiaki rawa i a tātou. Mai i te 11:59pm i te 25 o Kohitātea 2021, katoa ngā tāngata e haere mai ana ki Aotearoa, hāunga anō ērā o Ahitereiria, o Anatātika, o Rarotonga, o ngā Moutere o Maikoronihia, o Whīti, o Kiripati, o ngā Moutere Māhara, o Nauru, o Niu Karetōnia, o Niue, o Parau, o Hāmoa, o ngā Motu Horomona, o Tokerau, o Tonga, o Tuwaru, o Whenuatū, o Uwea me Whutuna, me mātua whakamātautau mō te KOWHEORI-19, ā, me korona-kore te whakatau a te whakamātautau, e 72 hāora i mua i te wehetanga, ka mutu ka whakaatu mai hoki i te tiwhikete taiwhanga pūtaiao, i tētahi atu momo taunakitanga tōtika rānei. E whakaaetia ana hoki te katoa o ngā whakamātau PCR , whakamātau LAMP me ngā whakamātau kita whakamate mō tēnei whakamātau tōmua. Me mahi atu ngā whakamātautau katoa e tētahi taiwhanga pūtaiao. E whakaaetia ana hoki ngā tiwhikete tohuora kua tuhia ki reo kē. E whakawāteatia ana i te whakamātau tōmua ko ngā tamariki kāore anō kia rua tau (24 marama) te pakeke. E whakawāteatia ana i te whakamātau tōmua ko te tangata haere mai ki Aotearoa he tiwhikete tohuora tāna e tohu ana kua ora ake ia i te KOWHEORI-19, e kore hoki e pāngia tētahi atu ki taua mate e ia. Ko ngā tāngata haere kāore e taea te whakamātau nā tētahi take hauora, me mātua toro ki tētahi tākuta i roto i te 72 hāora i mua i tō wehetanga. Me mātua homai e te tākuta he tiwhikete tohuora e whakaatu ana he take hauora kē i kore ai koe e whakamātauria, ā, kāore hoki ō tohumate KOWHEORI-19. Mēnā e rere ana koe ki whenua kē mā Aotearoa, ā, kāore koe e puta i te taiwhanga whakawhiti waka rererangi, e whakawāteatia ana koe i te whakamātau tōmua. E kaha ana te whakahau ki te hunga haere kia whakapā atu ki ō rātou kamupene rererangi kei tūpono he whakaritenga anō ā rātou mō ngā whakamātau tōmua. Me mōhio anō hoki ki ngā whakaritenga a ērā atu whenua e whakawhiti atu ai rātou. Mai i te 8 o Huitanguru, katoa ngā pāhihi ka tae mai ki Aotearoa (i tua atu i ērā nō ngā whenua i whakawāteatia), kāore he tohu whakaatu i te korenga o te KOWHEORI-19, tēnā rānei he tiwhikete tohuora, tērā pea e whiua ki te whaina, piki atu ki te $1,000. Hei te taunga mai ki Aotearoa, ko ngā tāngata haere mai katoa: me noho ki tētahi puni whakamohoao, whaitua taratahi rānei mō te 14 rā me whakamātau mō te KOWHEORI-19 i te rā 0 (arā, i te rā tonu e tae atu ai ki te puni whakamohoao) me noho ki tōna ake rūma kia mōhiotia rā anō te whakatau a te whakamātautau me he tohumate korona i te taenga mai o te tangata, ka haere tōtika atu ki tētahi whaitua taratahi. He werohanga ihu PCR te momo whakamātautau nei. Ka 24-28 hāora kia hoki mai ngā whakataunga whakamātautau. Me he korona-kore te whakatau a te whakamātautau, ka noho tonu te tangata ki te puni whakamohoao mō te roanga atu o ngā rā 14. Ka whakamātauria anō i te takiwā o te rā 3 me te rā 12 o tā rātou noho. Mō te katoa tonu o ngā tāngata, me korona-kore te whakatau a te whakamātautau KOWHEORI-19 me whakaae hoki e tō mātou kāhui hauora he iti te tūpono kei te kawea haere te mate korona, kua pāngia rānei ki ētahi atu kātahi anō ka whakaaetia te wehe atu i te puni whakamohoao. Mehemea he mate korona te whakatau, ka tōmua ake te neke i te tangata ki te whaitua taratahi, tēnā i kore ai te whakamātautau i te rā 0. Hei tūwatawata anō te whakamātautau o te rā 0 hei ārai atu i a KOWHEORI-19 i Aotearoa, tae atu ki ōna putanga kētanga hou kua ara ake i tāwāhi, me te tere ake o te horapa haere. Mō ngā tino kōrero o te wā e pā ana ki te mate korona, tēnā peka ki https://covid19.govt.nz/updates-and-resources/translations/ Mō ētahi atu kōrero e pā ana ki ngā puni whakamohoao, me ngā whaitua taratahi, haere ki tēnei: https://www.miq.govt.nz/travel-to-new-zealand/arriving-in-nz/ (external link) --- Section Separator --- Ko te pare atu i te mate korona i Aotearoa, te mahi tiaki rawa i a tātou. Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori Te Taratahi-Kore o te Hāereere i waenga i Aotearoa me Ahitereiria | Quarantine-Free Travel between N --- Section Separator --- Kua āhei te Taratahi-Kore o tō hāereere i waenga i Aotearoa me Ahitereiria, me te kore e mate ki te Noho Whakataratahi. E Taratahi-Kore ai te rere, me kaua e iti iho i te 14 rā te roa o tō noho ki Aotearoa rānei, ki Ahitereiria rānei, ka mutu me eke ngā paearu whakauru. Tērā pea ka tere tonu te huringa o ēnei paearu i muri tata i te pānuitanga. E ū tonu ana ki ngā ture mō te manene - mehemea me whai kōkota i te nuinga o te wā e uru ai koe ki Ahitereiria rānei, ki Aotearoa rānei, me whai tonu e koe ināianei. Ka rerekē te āhua o te hāereere i tērā e taunga nei koe - ka kite koe i ngā kiringaio hauora e mahi ana i ngā mātai ā-hauora, ka mutu me mau koe i tētahi tākai mata i te waka rererangi. Me whakautu pātai hoki koe mō tōu hauora i te wehenga - mehemea kua pāngia koe e ngā tohumate o te mate romahā me te rewharewha kāore e āhei tō hāereere. Me mātua oti i a koe tētahi whakapuakanga hāereere i mua i te paunga o te 72 hāora i mua i tō wehenga i Aotearoa ( www.covid19.homeaffairs.gov.au/australia-travel-declaration (external link) ). Me mātua mōhio hoki koe e whakaae ana te takiwā ā-mana motuhake, te takiwā ā-mana karauna rānei e haere nā koe ki ngā rerenga Taratahi-Kore i Aotearoa. Tirohia he pārongo atu anō mō te haere ki Ahitereiria (external link) He pārongo hāereere mō ia takiwā ā-mana motuhake/mana karauna: Australian Capital Territory (external link) New South Wales (external link) Northern Territory (external link) Queensland (external link) South Australia (external link) Tasmania (external link) Victoria (external link) Western Australia (external link) Me mātua oti i a koe tētahi whakapuakanga ā-ipurangi mō te hāereere i mua i tō wehenga i Ahitereiria ( naumaira.covid19.govt.nz/ (external link) ). Ki te pakaru mai te mate ki Ahitereiria i a koe i reira, ka mate pea koe ki te noho whakataratahi i tō taenga ki Aotearoa. Me utu koe i tō noho ki reira. Tirohia he pārongo atu anō mō te haere ki Aotearoa Tirohia te āhua o te whakahaerehia o tētahi kua pāngia e KOWHEORI-19 i Ahitereiria --- Section Separator --- Kua āhei te Taratahi-Kore o tō hāereere i waenga i Aotearoa me Ahitereiria, me te kore e mate ki te Noho Whakataratahi. Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori He Pūtea Āwhina i Ngā Kaipakihi | Financial support for businesses --- Section Separator --- Kua whakaritea e Te Hiranga Tangata he Tauwaea Whakaara ( 0800 559 009 ) hei manaaki i ngā hapori kua raru nei. Tērā ētahi āwhinatanga kaipakihi a Te Hiranga Tangata hei torotoro. Mēnā kua kīia kia noho whakamohoao ō kaimahi, ā, kāore hoki e taea te mahi i te kāinga, ka taea e koe te tono pūtea hei utu tonu i a rātou. He pārongo mō tētahi Pūtea Āwhina hou hei āwhina i ngā kaipakihi kua heke nei ā rātou moni whiwhi i runga i te huringa o ngā Pae Mataara Mate Korona. Utu Ngaronga Wā Poto – E wātea ana te Utu Ngaronga Wā Poto Mate Korona ki ngā kaipakihi, tae atu hoki ki te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō, hei āwhina ki te utu i ō rātou kaimahi kāore nei e taea te mahi i te kāinga i a rātou e tatari ana kia whakahokia mai ō rātou whakamātaunga Mate Korona. Kaupapa Āwhina Rangi Whakatā – E whai wāhi ana ki te Kaupapa Āwhina Rangi Whakatā ko ngā kaimahi e rite ana, tae atu hoki ki te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō, kāore e taea te mahi i te kāinga, ā, kua pāngia nei e te momo māuiui, hei tauira, kua pāngia e te Mate Korona, kua kīia ai rānei he ‘hoa tata’, ā, me noho whakamohoao ki te kāinga mō ngā rā 14. Pūtea Whakaara – He mea āwhina te Pūtea Whakaara a Te Tari Tāke i ngā kaipakihi kua raru nei i te nui haere o ngā putanga Pae Mataara. Kei te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata (external link) ngā kōrero mō te Pūtea Āwhina, te Utu Ngaronga Wā Poto, me te Kaupapa Āwhina Rangi Whakatā. Kei te pae tukutuku o Te Tari Tāke (external link) ngā kōrero mō te Pūtea Whakaara. He āwhinatanga kei te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata, whakapā atu ki te pokapū i 0800 559 009 me MyMSD E puare ana ngā pokapū o Te Hiranga Tangata i ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2, e katia ana i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4. Ka whakahaeretia ā-waeahia ngā whakaritenga i raro i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4, i ngā wā e rite ana. Ka rite tonu ngā whakaritenga mō ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2. Ka utua tonutia ngā utu e rite ana e Te Hiranga Tangata. Ka whakamāramatia ngā utu e wātea ana i te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata (external link) . Kei te wātea hoki ēnei utu mō te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō. --- Section Separator --- Kua whakaritea e Te Hiranga Tangata he Tauwaea Whakaara ( 0800 559 009 ) hei manaaki i ngā hapori kua raru nei. Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori Hei āwhina tangata | Support for individuals --- Section Separator --- Ki te kore e taea e koe te wehe i tō kāinga ki te tiki kai, me whai kia: Tīkina he kai e tō whānau, e ō hoa rānei. Tonoa he kai i te ipurangi i tō hokomaha mā tā rātou ratonga mā te hunga me mātua whai āwhina. Tērā tonu pea ka whai āwhina koe i Te Hiranga Tangata. Ehara i te mea me kiritaki kē koe nā Te Hiranga Tangata. Waeahia te 0800 559 009 Go to MyMSD (external link) Ki te totoa tō hiahia ki te whai kai i ngā hāora e 24-48 e whai ake nei, e pai ana hoki tō whakapā atu ki tētahi putunga kai o te rohe pātata. Rapua ngā putunga kai me ētahi atu ratonga tuku kai puta noa i Aotearoa (external link) He āwhinatanga kei te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata, whakapā atu ki te pokapū i 0800 559 009 me MyMSD. E puare ana ngā pokapū o Te Hiranga Tangata i ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2, e katia ana i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4. Ka whakahaeretia ā-waeahia ngā whakaritenga i raro i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4, i ngā wā e rite ana. Ka whakahaeretia ngā whakaritenga i raro i ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2 i ngā pokapū o Te Hiranga Tangata. Ka utua tonutia ngā utu e rite ana e Te Hiranga Tangata. Mēnā kua tonoa koe kia noho whakamohoao me te kore e āhei ki te mahi i te kāinga, me kōrero ki tō kaitukumahi. Tērā pea ka taea e ia te tono kia whiwhi moni hei utu tonu i a koe. Ka whakamāramatia ngā utu e wātea ana i te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata (external link) . Kei te wātea hoki ēnei utu mō te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō. Mēnā kāore e taea e koe te mahi i te kāinga i a koe e tatari ana ki tō whakamātaunga Mate Korona, ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono kia utua kotahitia mai te $350 hei utu tonu i a koe. Kei te wātea hoki tēnei utu mō te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō. Mēnā kāore e taea e koe te mahi i te kāinga i a koe e noho whakamohoao ana ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono ki te Kaupapa Āwhina Rangi Whakatā. Ka kotahi putunga mai te utu ki ngā kaitukumahi, ā, ka utua mō te rua wiki mō ia kaimahi e whai wāhi mai ana, $585.80 mō ia kaimahi e mahi ana mō ngā haora 20 neke atu i ia wiki, ka $350 mō ia kaimahi e mahi ana mō ngā haora i raro i te 20 i ia wiki. Mēnā kua raru tō wāhi mahi i te huringa Pae Mataara, ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono ki te pūtea āwhina me te pūtea whakaara hei utu i a koe, kia whai mahi tonu koe. Mēnā kua poroa tō tūranga mahi, kua whakahekea rānei ō hāora mahi, he āwhina kei Te Hiranga Tangata mō te taha ki ngā utu totoa pēnei i ō te: kai utu noho whare, hei tauira, ko te reti, ko te mōkete ranei, ko te reti rūma, ko te whawhati tata o te whakarite whare, ko te hūnuku whare tapitapi, i ō te whakahou rānei i ngā taputapu ā-whare whawhati tata o te whai rongoā ā-niho whawhati tata o e whai rongoā ā-hauora whakakī kurawai. Te tautoko ā-pūtea, ngā paearu whai wāhi me te ara hei tono, i te pae tukutuku a Te Hiranga Tangata (external link) Whakapā atu rānei ki Te Hiranga Tangata i; Te 0800 559 009 Ngā kaumātua e pakeke ake ana i te 65 tau: 0800 552 002 , ko tēnei tau rānei +64 4 978 1180 Ngā tauira: 0800 88 99 00 www.studylink.govt.nz (external link) E āhei ana tā te hunga turi, tā te hunga kāore e rongo tika ana, tā te hunga kāore hoki e mārama ana te kōrero whakamahi i te Deaf Link i runga i te kore utu Waea whakaahuahia te 0800 621 621 Pātuhihia te 029 286 7170 MSD_Deaf_Services@msd.govt.nz WorkSafe 0800 030 040 , ko tēnei rānei +64 4 897 7699 www.worksafe.govt.nz (external link) www.employment.govt.nz (external link) waeahia rānei te 0800 20 90 20 , tēnei rānei +64 9 969 2950 Te hunga reti 0800 646 483 www.hud.govt.nz (external link) īmērahia rānei te info@hud.govt.nz Ngā ratonga whare taupua 0508 754 163 https://temporaryaccommodation.mbie.govt.nz (external link) Waeahia te tau whawhati tata o te 111 mēnā e inamata ana te mōrearea ōu, o tētahi atu rānei  i te tūkino mai a tētahi, i te hiahia rānei o tētahi ki te tūkino i a ia anō. E hono ai koe ki ngā ratonga tautoko ā-pāpori i tō rohe pātata, waeahia te tau whai āwhina, 211 nei, o Ngā Ratonga ā-Whānau, te 0800 211 211 , toro atu rānei ki www.familyservices.govt.nz/directory/ (external link) He kupu ārahi, he tautoko, he whare haumaru hoki kei Te Punanga Wāhine mēnā kei te pā mai ngā mahi tūkino a tētahi ki tōu ao. 0800 733 843 He ratonga utu-kore te Tau-āwhina o Te Tūkino Kaumātua e wātea ana ki ngā kaumātua mēnā kei te tūkinotia rātou, kei te tūkinotia rānei tētahi atu e mōhiotia ana e rātou. 0800 32 668 65 E whai tautoko ai koe mō te mānukanuka, mō te ahotea, mō te oranga rānei o te hinengaro, waeahia, pātuhihia rānei te 1737 ki te kōrero ki tētahi kua whakangungua ki te āwhina, kāore nei he utu, i ngā hāora e 24 i ia rā, i ngā rā e 7 o te wiki. E pai ana hoki tō whakapā atu ki te Tau-āwhina mō te Hinapōuri, ki te 0800 111 757 ki te Tau-āwhina hoki mō te Waipiro me te Whakapōauau, ki te 0800 787 797 . --- Section Separator --- Ki te kore e taea e koe te wehe i tō kāinga ki te tiki kai, me whai kia: Tīkina he kai e tō whānau, e ō hoa rānei. Tonoa he kai i te ipurangi i tō hokomaha mā tā rātou ratonga mā te hunga me mātua whai āwhina. Tērā tonu pea ka whai āwhina koe i Te Hiranga Tangata. Ehara i te mea me kiritaki kē koe nā Te Hiranga Tangata. Waeahia te 0800 559 009 Go to MyMSD (external link) Ki te totoa tō hiahia ki te whai kai i ngā hāora e 24-48 e whai ake nei, e pai ana hoki tō whakapā atu ki tētahi putunga kai o te rohe pātata. Rapua ngā putunga kai me ētahi atu ratonga tuku kai puta noa i Aotearoa (external link) He āwhinatanga kei te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata, whakapā atu ki te pokapū i 0800 559 009 me MyMSD. E puare ana ngā pokapū o Te Hiranga Tangata i ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2, e katia ana i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4. Ka whakahaeretia ā-waeahia ngā whakaritenga i raro i ngā Pae Mataara 3 me te 4, i ngā wā e rite ana. Ka whakahaeretia ngā whakaritenga i raro i ngā Pae Mataara 1 me te 2 i ngā pokapū o Te Hiranga Tangata. Ka utua tonutia ngā utu e rite ana e Te Hiranga Tangata. Mēnā kua tonoa koe kia noho whakamohoao me te kore e āhei ki te mahi i te kāinga, me kōrero ki tō kaitukumahi. Tērā pea ka taea e ia te tono kia whiwhi moni hei utu tonu i a koe. Ka whakamāramatia ngā utu e wātea ana i te pae tukutuku o Te Hiranga Tangata (external link) . Kei te wātea hoki ēnei utu mō te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō. Mēnā kāore e taea e koe te mahi i te kāinga i a koe e tatari ana ki tō whakamātaunga Mate Korona, ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono kia utua kotahitia mai te $350 hei utu tonu i a koe. Kei te wātea hoki tēnei utu mō te hunga whakawhiwhi mahi mō rātou anō. Mēnā kāore e taea e koe te mahi i te kāinga i a koe e noho whakamohoao ana ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono ki te Kaupapa Āwhina Rangi Whakatā. Ka kotahi putunga mai te utu ki ngā kaitukumahi, ā, ka utua mō te rua wiki mō ia kaimahi e whai wāhi mai ana, $585.80 mō ia kaimahi e mahi ana mō ngā haora 20 neke atu i ia wiki, ka $350 mō ia kaimahi e mahi ana mō ngā haora i raro i te 20 i ia wiki. Mēnā kua raru tō wāhi mahi i te huringa Pae Mataara, ka taea e tō kaitukumahi te tono ki te pūtea āwhina me te pūtea whakaara hei utu i a koe, kia whai mahi tonu koe. Mēnā kua poroa tō tūranga mahi, kua whakahekea rānei ō hāora mahi, he āwhina kei Te Hiranga Tangata mō te taha ki ngā utu totoa pēnei i ō te: kai utu noho whare, hei tauira, ko te reti, ko te mōkete ranei, ko te reti rūma, ko te whawhati tata o te whakarite whare, ko te hūnuku whare tapitapi, i ō te whakahou rānei i ngā taputapu ā-whare whawhati tata o te whai rongoā ā-niho whawhati tata o e whai rongoā ā-hauora whakakī kurawai. Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori Te whakamātautau | Testing --- Section Separator --- Mehemea kua pāngia koe e ngā tohumate o te maremare, o te mate rānei e pēnei ana i te rewharewha, e noho ki te kāinga, ka waea-utukore ai ki Healthline mā te 0800 358 5453, ki tō whare hauora ā-iwi rānei, ki tō tākuta rānei ki te tuku pātai e pā ana ki te whakamātautau. Kāore he utu o te whakamātautau. E mau ai te wheori i waenga i ō tātou hapori, me whakamātautau rawa te tangata kua pāngia e ngā tohumate o te KOWHEORI-19. Kāore he utu o te whakamātautanga, o te tapuhitanga rānei e pā ana ki te KOWHEORI-19, ka mutu e wātea ana ki te katoa o ngā tāngata o Aotearoa, tae atu ki ērā kāore nei ō rātou kōkota whaimana ā-ture. Tēnā, hoatu ō taipitopito whakapānga ki te hunga e whakahaere ana i te whakamātautau kia whakapā ai rātou ki a koe e pā ana ki ngā hua o te whakamātautau. Ehara i te mea me whai nama Tautuhi Hauora ā-Motu ( NHI ) koe, me whakaatu rānei tō tohu tautuhi e whakamātauhia ai koe. He rite tonu te panonihia o ngā wāhi e whakamātauria ai koe. Ko te wāhi pai katoa e kitea ai tētahi rārangi o te wā, ko tō Poari Hauora ā-Rohe e pātata ana, ko ngā Whare Hauora Tūmatanui rānei e pātata ana. Kei raro iho nei ētahi o aua pārongo: Te Tai Tokerau (external link) Tāmaki-makaurau (external link) Waikato (external link) Waiariki, Rotorua me Taupō (external link) Upoko ki te Uru Hauora (external link) Te Awakairangi (external link) Te Wairarapa (external link) Te Matau a Māui (external link) Whakatāne (external link) Te Pae Hauora o Tararua, o Ruahine (Ōtaki, Taitoko, Papaioea, Kawakawa, Tāmaki-nui-a-Rua) (external link) Te Tairāwhiti (Tūranga) (external link) Taranaki (external link) Waitematā (external link) Whanganui (external link) Waitaha (external link) Te Waiora (external link) Waitaha ki te Tonga (external link) Te Tonga (external link) Te Poari Hauora ā-Rohe o Tai Poutini (external link) Mehemea me whakamātautau koe e pā ana ki te KOWHEORI-19, he tīpakotanga nō tō tinana ka tangohia. Ko te huarahi e auau katoa ana te whāia, ko te muku i te pakohu o tō ihu. He rite te rāmuku ki te matahune, engari he roa ake te rākau. Ka tukuna te tīpakotanga ki tētahi taiwhanga pūtaiao kia tātarihia. Ka pau pea tētahi wā roa tonu, kātahi ngā hua mai i te taiwhanga pūtaiao ka puta. Ina whakamātauria koe, ka kīia atu ki a koe te wā me te āhua e tau ai ki a koe ngā hua mōu. Mehemea kei Tāmaki-makaurau tō kāinga, me mātua noho koe ki te kāinga noho taratahi ai, tae noa ki te wā ka tau ki a koe ngā hua mōu. Ehara i te mea me noho taratahi te nuinga o ngā tāngata kei waho o Tāmaki-makaurau e noho ana i te wā e tāria ana te hua o te whakamātautau — mā tō tākuta koe hei tohutohu e pā ana ki tēnei take. Ka mātua tonoa koe kia noho taratahi mehemea: kua hoki mai koe i tāwāhi i nā tata nei kua pā atu koe ki tētahi kua hoki mai i tāwāhi i nā tata nei he whakapānga tata koe nō tētahi kua pāngia e te KOWHEORI-19. Mehemea ka whakamātauhia koe, tēnā, whāia ngā tohutohu ki a koe e pā ana ki ngā mahi ka whai ake. Tērā pea, ka āwangawanga koe, ka nui rānei ō pātai mehemea ka tau ki a koe tētahi hua whakamātautau e tohu ana i te pāngia ōu e te KOWHEORI-19. Ka waeahia koe e tētahi kaimahi hauora ki te kōrero mō ngā pānga o tēnei take ki a koutou ko tō whānau. Kei reira taua kaimahi hei tautoko, hei āwhina hoki i a koe. Ka kōrero ia ki a koe e pā ana ki te katoa kua whakapāngia e koe i nā tata nei. Ka kōrero hoki ia ki a koe e pā ana ki te nuku i a koe — i a koutou rānei ko tō whānau, ki te hiahia koe kia pērā - ki tētahi wāhi whakataratahi (external link) kia eke ai te tapuhitanga o koutou katoa ki te taumata tiketike katoa ka taea, ā, kia kaua ai hoki te wheori e hōrapa. Ka noho koutou katoa ki tētahi wāhi kotahi, engari ki te māuiui koe ka noho pea koe ki tētahi rūma kē atu i ō tō whānau kāore nei i te māuiui. Ki te hiahia tō whānau ki te noho taratahi ki te kāinga, tēnā i te haere ki te wāhi whakataratahi, e pai ana tēnā. Ko te whāinga hoki, kia eke te haumarutanga o te katoa ki tōna taumata tiketike katoa ka taea. Kāore he utu o ngā ratonga whakataratahi katoa, pēnei i ngā kai, i ngā timotimo kai, i te ipurangi here-kore, i te horoi kaka, i ngā taputapu horoi tinana me mātua whai me ngā inu. Mehemea ka māuiui koe, mā tētahi rōpū hauora kua āta tohua koe hei tapuhi. Mehemea ka pāngia te tamaiti, tōna whānau rānei e tiaki ana i a ia e te KOWHEORI-19, ā, me mātua whakataratahi, ka āta whakaū mātou i te haumaru o te noho a te tamaiti ki ngā ringa manaaki o tōna whānau. Ka āhei tō wehenga atu ā tōna wā e piki ai te ora ki a koe. --- Section Separator --- Mehemea kua pāngia koe e ngā tohumate o te maremare, o te mate rānei e pēnei ana i te rewharewha, e noho ki te kāinga, ka waea-utukore ai ki Healthline mā te 0800 358 5453, ki tō whare hauora ā-iwi rānei, ki tō tākuta rānei ki te tuku pātai e pā ana ki te whakamātautau. Ka kōrero hoki ia ki a koe e pā ana ki te nuku i a koe — i a koutou rānei ko tō whānau, ki te hiahia koe kia pērā - ki tētahi wāhi whakataratahi (external link) kia eke ai te tapuhitanga o koutou katoa ki te taumata tiketike katoa ka taea, ā, kia kaua ai hoki te wheori e hōrapa. Ka noho koutou katoa ki tētahi wāhi kotahi, engari ki te māuiui koe ka noho pea koe ki tētahi rūma kē atu i ō tō whānau kāore nei i te māuiui. Ki te hiahia tō whānau ki te noho taratahi ki te kāinga, tēnā i te haere ki te wāhi whakataratahi, e pai ana tēnā. Ko te whāinga hoki, kia eke te haumarutanga o te katoa ki tōna taumata tiketike katoa ka taea. Kāore he utu o ngā ratonga whakataratahi katoa, pēnei i ngā kai, i ngā timotimo kai, i te ipurangi here-kore, i te horoi kaka, i ngā taputapu horoi tinana me mātua whai me ngā inu. Mehemea ka māuiui koe, mā tētahi rōpū hauora kua āta tohua koe hei tapuhi. Mehemea ka pāngia te tamaiti, tōna whānau rānei e tiaki ana i a ia e te KOWHEORI-19, ā, me mātua whakataratahi, ka āta whakaū mātou i te haumaru o te noho a te tamaiti ki ngā ringa manaaki o tōna whānau. Ka āhei tō wehenga atu ā tōna wā e piki ai te ora ki a koe. --- Section Separator --- Te reo Māori Te whakamātau tōmua i te hunga e haere mai ana ki Aotearoa | Pre-departure testing for travellers to Home Updates and resources Translations Te reo Māori Whakakā i te kimi Hono iarere | Turn on Bluetooth tracing --- Section Separator --- Kua whakahoutia te taupānga NZ COVID Tracer ki te hangarau kimi Hono iarere. Mā te kimi Hono iarere e āhei ai tō whiwhi i tētahi whakaohiti mēnā kua whakapā tata koe ki tētahi atu kaiwhakamahi taupānga ka pāngia e te KOWHEORI-19. Ehara i te mea whakakapi te kimi Hono iarere i ngā tukanga kimi pāpātanga o nāianei, i ngā waehere QR NZ COVID Tracer rānei. Kei te whai tikanga tonu te mahi matawai i ngā waehere QR ki te aroturuki i ō haerenga. He mea tāpiri te utauta kimi Hono iarere — māna e āwhina ki te kimi tāngata kua whakapā tata mai ki a tātou. Mā te whakakā tonu i te kimi Hono iarere, ka tukuna tētahi waehere ID tupurangi, he matatapu, he haumaru. He rite ki te papakitanga a ngā ringa ā-matihiko i waenga i ngā waea kawe kei te pā tata mai. Mā te āheinga kimi e hopu ai i pēhea nei te tata mai a tētahi atu waea, ā, i pēhea nei te roa. Ko ngā waea ka whakapā mai me kā mai anō te kimi Hono iarere hoki. Mā tēnei e kite ai ina pāngia ai tētahi ki te KOWHEORI-19, ka āhei ia ki te tuku i tētahi whakamōhiotanga kirimuna ko ngā waehere ID tupurangi kei roto i ngā mea kua tukuna atu e ngā waea kawe i roto i ngā rā 14 kua hori. Ki te mōhio tō waea ki tētahi o ēnei waehere ID kua whakapā tata rawa ki a koe, ka mutu, kua roa tō noho atu mō te tūpono pāngia e te mate, ka whiwhi whakaohiti koe. Mā tēnei whakaohiti koe e tohutohu ki ngā mahi e noho haumaru ai koe me tō whānau. Mātakitaki i te kiriata kimi Hono iarere i tēnei whārangi kia kitea ai tana mahi. (external link) Ko tā te nuinga o ngā waea kawe he whakahou aunoa i te taupānga. Ka āhei hoki koe ki te whakahou ake ā-ringa i te taupānga i te toa taupānga, i te toa pūrei rānei. Kia whakahou ake rawa, mā te taupānga koe e ui mēnā me whakakā ake te kimi Hono iarere. Ka kā rawa mai, ka mahi tonu i tāna mahi ahakoa kua kati te taupānga. Kāore te kimi Hono iarere e whakamahi i ngā raraunga kawekawe, kāore hoki e whakamimiti i te pūhiko nā te mea he Ngao Iti Hono iarere. Mā tō whakahohe i te kimi Hono iarere, ka tiakina tō matatapu i ngā wā katoa — kāore e taea te whakaatu tō tauwāhi, tō ingoa, ētahi kōrero rānei e pā ana ki a koe. Kāore hoki te Hono iarere e hopu ko wai mā i whakapā tata mai, ā, i whea rānei koe. Ko te tikanga mēnā ka whiwhi koe i tētahi whakaohiti inā hoki kua whakapā tata koe ki tētahi atu kua pāngia e te KOWHEORI-19, kāore he tāngata i tua atu i a koe e mōhio kua riro i a koe. Ko ngā mōhiohio katoa a te kimi pāpātanga kua hopukina ki te taupānga ka mau mārika ki tō waea kawe, ā, kei a koe te tikanga i ngā wā katoa ki te āhua o ngā mōhiohio ka tohua e koe hei tuari. --- Section Separator --- Kua whakahoutia te taupānga NZ COVID Tracer ki te hangarau kimi Hono iarere. Home Updates and resources Unstoppable summer toolkit --- Section Separator --- Everyone wants an endless summer. Those long glorious days that roll into weeks. No one wants it cut short. And to make sure it isn’t, we all need to do our bit. We need to show New Zealand that washing their hands, scanning QR codes, turning on Bluetooth tracing and staying home if they’re sick is the best way to unite and make our summer unstoppable. Warning: video contains flashing images. Please look away if you have a history of photosensitive epilepsy or suffer from migraines. Unstoppable summer: A COVID-19 public service announcement (Original) Unstoppable summer: A COVID-19 public service announcement (Short version) To help to make summer unstoppable, we have developed a music track featuring Dr Ashley Bloomfield. This video is available to use at events and festivals. If you would like the raw video files, please contact us at covid.comms@dpmc.govt.nz Order collateral to help your business, organisation or event make summer unstoppable.
